### PRO TOUR KHANS OF TARKIR


TOP STANDARD DECKS O-Z
======================



![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)

Wizards of the Coast




October 12, 2014
 











 Listed below are all the Standard decks that earned 21 points or more in the Constructed rounds of Pro Tour *Khans of Tarkir*. Each deck is preceded by a short explanation of how the deck works.




**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.







#### Oliver Oks


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-13cca4118b4dcd6ea0f802df34804b2d.txt?n=Oliver%20Oks)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Seeker+of+the+Way)


















**Esper Control**




 Esper Control utilizes almost all of the most powerful control spells the format has to offer, going into white for [End Hostilities](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=End+Hostilities) and some forms of life-gain. [Resolute Archangel](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Resolute+Archangel) and [Nyx-Fleece Ram](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Nyx-Fleece+Ram) keep your life total high.







#### Gregory Orange


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-0e58f6428a9a55e47dfaa96fec791ff4.txt?n=Gregory%20Orange)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Elspeth%2C+Sun%27s+Champion)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### David Palmer


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-081cb290273c3b472f8aad94899374ce.txt?n=David%20Palmer)

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.







#### Jamie Parke


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-4112d7696acbac4296417019217529d6.txt?n=Jamie%20Parke)

**Black-Green Devotion**




 These green-based devotion decks try to take advantage of all of the mana that can be generated by [Nykthos, Shrine to Nyx](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Nykthos%2C+Shrine+to+Nyx). There is often a small constellation sub-theme, with black helping out via removal.







#### Ruben Perez


#####

**Red-White Tokens**




[Hordeling Outburst](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Hordeling+Outburst) and [Goblin Rabblemaster](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Goblin+Rabblemaster) team up with [Monastery Swiftspear](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Monastery+Swiftspear) and a large helping of burn to quickly drop the opponent to zero.

**Blue-Black Control**




 A pure control strategy, this two-color deck wants to remove all of the opponent's threats one-by-one, pulling ahead on cards with [Dig Through Time](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Dig+Through+Time) and [Jace's Ingenuity](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jace%27s+Ingenuity). [Perilous Vault](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Perilous+Vault) is the sweeper of choice, and can reset virtually any board to the control player's favor.







#### Adrian Sullivan


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-ec612bdaa0105f48ce8b3ff393c449cc.txt?n=Adrian%20Sullivan)

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Goblin+Rabblemaster)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Bram Snepvangers


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-b0b69484118cc9b38bf28dddd247d48f.txt?n=Bram%20Snepvangers)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Fleecemane+Lion)


















**Abzan Aggro**




 This more aggressive take on Abzan often forgoes [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid) and [Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) for more aggressively-minded creatures, such as [Rakshasa Deathdealer](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Rakshasa+Deathdealer) and [Herald of Torment](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Herald+of+Torment), trying to put opponents off balance with some of the strongest creatures at every point in the curve.







#### Mike Sigrist


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-9a455889da29825f4c5517f08bc96514.txt?n=Mike%20Sigrist)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Fleecemane+Lion)


















**Jeskai Ascendancy Combo**




 The format's only true combo deck, [Jeskai Ascendancy](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jeskai+Ascendancy) uses its namesake card along with creatures that make mana to churn through its deck, casting spell after spell before ultimately killing with a large attacking creature, decking from [Altar of the Brood](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Altar+of+the+Brood), or any number of ways. [Retraction Helix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Retraction+Helix) and a zero-cost spell make the combo repeatable as many times as necessary.







#### Lee Shi Tian


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-90a1e1fbd1be1917e2ff46c33a7aef22.txt?n=Lee%20Shi%20Tian)

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.







#### Alexey Shashov

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Seeker+of+the+Way)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Matt Severa


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-21de2bc75e965cad98a2dff0c1edaa46.txt?n=Matt%20Severa)

**Blue-Black Control**




 A pure control strategy, this two-color deck wants to remove all of the opponent's threats one-by-one, pulling ahead on cards with [Dig Through Time](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Dig+Through+Time) and [Jace's Ingenuity](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jace%27s+Ingenuity). [Perilous Vault](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Perilous+Vault) is the sweeper of choice, and can reset virtually any board to the control player's favor.







#### Owen Turtenwald


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-ac49181815c53e6115809af5c54ccbd4.txt?n=Owen%20Turtenwald)

**Black-Green Devotion**




 These green-based devotion decks try to take advantage of all of the mana that can be generated by [Nykthos, Shrine to Nyx](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Nykthos%2C+Shrine+to+Nyx). There is often a small constellation sub-theme, with black helping out via removal.







#### Felipe Tapia Becerra

**Unwritten Devotion**




 This green and black devotion deck utilizes [Nykthos, Shrine to Nyx](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Nykthos%2C+Shrine+to+Nyx) to make a ton of mana, supports a constellation sub-theme, AND goes for the big score with [See the Unwritten](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=See+the+Unwritten).







#### Gaudenis Vidugiris


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a1cb9c45c4f5661c0e23fe0cc7f0a2e3.txt?n=Gaudenis%20Vidugiris)

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Don van Ravenszaaij


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-2ba20505360a9d7aa2d503c6e0e5dac5.txt?n=Don%20van%20Ravenszaaij)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Forest)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Steve Wise


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-1e72db5aa4fc617a7aca36425c54b506.txt?n=Steve%20Wise)

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.







#### Julian Wildes

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.

**Red-Green Monsters**




 The deck uses mana acceleration to quickly pump out some of the biggest, scariest creatures in the format, helped out by a few of the biggest, scariest Planeswalkers in the Multiverse.







#### Benjamin Weitz

**Jeskai Wins**




 Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.







#### Yuuya Watanabe
